 467 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`register`**
 468 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`before_flush`**
 469 |       * âš¡ NOISE FILTER: Skip Outbox to prevent infinite loops
 470 | 
 471 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_process_object`**
 472 |       * **1.** âš¡ DYNAMIC DOMAIN RESOLUTION (No more hardcoded dicts)
 473 |       * We assume the domain matches the class name, unless overridden by the model itself.
 474 |       * Fallback for internal Kernel structures (Optional but safe)
 475 |       * **2.** âš¡ PRE-FLIGHT: Freeze & Calculate Changes
 476 |       * Construct default envelope
 477 |       * **3.** ðŸ§  THE BRAIN: GOVERNANCE ENGINE (Decoupled Sidecar)
 478 |       * Apply mutations if permitted
 479 |       * âš¡ FAIL-OPEN RESILIENCE: If Brain crashes, allow the body to survive.
 480 |       * **4.** ðŸƒ THE BODY: WORKFLOW ENGINE (Decoupled)
 481 |       * Need an ephemeral async session just to fetch state defs for the workflow engine
 482 |       * **5.** ðŸ¤ THE HANDSHAKE: Governance checks Workflow's Transition Request
 483 |       * Schedule side-effects (Actions)
 484 |       * **6.** âš¡ CHANGE DATA CAPTURE (CDC)
 485 |

 494 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/app/core/kernel/kernel.py`
 495 | **Components & Logic:**
 496 | 
 497 | - ðŸ“¦ **`Kernel`**
 498 |     > *The Event Publisher.*
 499 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`__init__`**
 500 |       * Stateless singleton pattern
 501 | 
 502 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`publish`**
 503 |       > *Ingests an event into the System Outbox.*
 504 |       * **1.** RESOLVE METADATA
 505 |       * **2.** RESOLVE CONTEXT
 506 |       * We grab the Trace ID from the request context to link API logs with Kafka logs
 507 |       * **3.** RESOLVE PARTITION KEY (Critical for Kafka)
 508 |       * If not provided, we try to use entity_id. If that's missing, we fallback to "global".
 509 |       * **WARNING:** "global" puts everything on one partition (ordering guaranteed but low throughput).
 510 |       * **4.** ENVELOPE CONSTRUCTION
 511 |       * **5.** WRITE TO OUTBOX
 512 |       * In Level 100, we DO raise. If the event cannot be logged, the transaction is unsafe.
 513 | 
 514 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`commit`**
 515 |       > *Finalizes the transaction.*

 781 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/app/core/meta/engine.py`
 782 | **Components & Logic:**
 783 | 
 784 | - ðŸ“¦ **`PolicyEngine`**
 785 |     > *The Universal Logic Executor.*
 786 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`evaluate`**
 787 |       > *The Main Entry Point.*
 788 |       * **1.** Prepare Data Context (Sandbox Envelope)
 789 |       * We wrap the data to allow 'context.meta' or 'context.actor' access if needed later.
 790 |       * Strategy: Pass object directly. Rules should be written as `host.weight > 10`.
 791 |       * **2.** Iterate Policies
 792 |       * **3.** Merge Results based on Governance Strategy
 793 |       * **4.** Apply Resolution Strategy ( The Judge )
 794 | 
 795 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_evaluate_single_policy`**
 796 |       > *Executes one Policy Bundle (which may contain multiple Rules).*
 797 |       * Policies store rules as a JSONB list: [{ "logic": "...", "action": "BLOCK", ... }]
 798 |       * A. Execute JMESPath
 799 |       * Boolean expressions: `host.age > 18` returns True/False.
 800 |       * B. Handle Match (Triggered)
 801 |       * âš¡ RESOLVE DYNAMIC VALUES
 802 |       * If action involves data, we must check if the value is a reference (e.g. actor.id)
 803 |       * **SAFEGUARD:** Bad rule syntax should not crash the system.
 804 |       * âš¡ FAIL OPEN: Treat crash as WARNING, not BLOCK.
 805 | 
 806 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_resolve_value`**
 807 |       > *Detects if a value is a reference (e.g. 'actor.id') and resolves it against the context.*
 808 |       * Heuristic: If it looks like a known context path, try to resolve it.
 809 |       * This matches the 'Value Source' logic in the Frontend Policy Editor.
 810 |       * If resolution works, return it. If it returns None, it might mean the field is missing,
 811 |       * but we return None rather than the string literal "actor.id".
 812 |       * If JMESPath crashes, fallback to the string literal
 813 | 
 814 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_apply_strategy`**
 815 |       > *Decides the final outcome based on the strategy.*
 816 |       * Default: Any violation kills the transaction
 817 |       * If (Total - Violations) > 0, then Pass.
 818 | 
 819 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_serialize`**
 820 |       > *Helper to convert SQLAlchemy objects to Dict for JMESPath.*
 821 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_log_summary`**
 822 |

 873 |       * **2.** Look for Transitions ('on' block)
 874 |       * **3.** Match Event

 877 |       * Short syntax: "EVENT": "TARGET"
 878 |       * Object syntax: "EVENT": { "target": "TARGET", "actions": [...] }
 879 |       * Array syntax (Guards): "EVENT": [{ "target": "T1", "guard": "cond" }]

1348 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/app/core/utilities/async_bridge.py`
1349 | **Components & Logic:**
1350 | 
1351 | - ðŸ“¦ **`AsyncBridge`**
1352 |     > *The Connector between the Blocking DB Layer and the Non-Blocking Logic Layer.*
1353 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`run_sync`**
1354 |       > *Executes a coroutine synchronously by spawning a fresh Event Loop in a separate thread.*
1355 |       * âš¡ 1. CAPTURE CONTEXT
1356 |       * Snapshot the current state (User, Request ID, etc.)
1357 |       * This allows the background thread to "know" who initiated the save.
1358 |       * âš¡ 2. SETUP SIDECAR LOOP
1359 |       * âš¡ 3. EXECUTE WITHIN CONTEXT
1360 |       * We wrap the execution in ctx.run() so the coroutine sees the vars.
1361 |       * Note: We must wrap the loop.run_until_complete call itself,
1362 |       * or create a wrapper task that runs in context.
1363 |       * Best practice: ctx.run(task)
1364 |       * The loop itself doesn't need the context, the coroutine does.
1365 |       * However, ctx.run() takes a callable.
1366 |       * We simply run the loop logic.
1367 |       * This ensures the async task inherits the context
1368 |       * But simpler: we just run the whole block in context if possible.
1369 |       * Actually, contextvars context applies to the *thread* execution stack.
1370 |       * So executing ctx.run(func) sets the context for 'func'.
1371 |       * âš¡ 4. SPAWN THREAD WITH CONTEXT
1372 |       * We pass 'target' to ctx.run, so 'target' runs with the variables set.
1373 |       * But we are starting a NEW thread. ctx.run() only works in the CURRENT thread.
1374 |       * To pass context to a NEW thread, we must run ctx.run INSIDE the new thread.
1375 |       * "Re-hydrate" the context inside the new thread
1376 |       * Block until the Sidecar finishes (Gatekeeper behavior)
1377 | 
1378 | 
1379 | ---
1380 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/app/core/utils/reflection.py`
1381 | **Components & Logic:**
1382 | 
1383 | - Æ’ **`reflect_model_schema`**
1384 |     > *Introspects a SQLAlchemy Model and returns a structured Context Graph.*
1385 |     * Indentation for logging readability
1386 |     * **1.** SCALAR FIELDS
1387 |     * âš¡ ARCHITECTURAL INVARIANT: Skip Dynamic Containers
1388 |     * The bucket itself is not a field, it holds the fields.
1389 |     * --- A. Type Mapping ---
1390 |     * Map SQLAlchemy Types to UI Types
1391 |     * --- B. Metadata Extraction (The Explicit Strategy) ---
1392 |     * We look for the 'info' dict on the column definition first.
1393 |     * Fallback to Heuristics if missing.
1394 |     * Label: Override or Auto-Generate
1395 |     * System/Read-Only Status
1396 |     * **1.** Explicit Override
1397 |     * **2.** Heuristic Fallback (Safety Net)
1398 |     * Final Decision Logic
1399 |     * Special Case: 'hashed_password'
1400 |     * Should be "password" widget, but never readable.
1401 |     * --- C. Construct Field Definition ---
1402 |     * Alias for logic engine
1403 |     * Placeholder for extended config
1404 |     * Inject options if found via Enum or Info
1405 |     * **2.** RELATIONSHIPS (The Graph)
1406 |     * Only recurse if we haven't hit the limit
1407 |     * Determine Cardinality
1408 |     * Recursive Call
1409 |     * **3.** CONSTRUCT OUTPUT

   7 |     constructor(message: string) {
   8 |         super(message);
   9 |         this.name = 'CancelError';
  10 |     }

  17 | export interface OnCancel {
  18 |     readonly isResolved: boolean;
  19 |     readonly isRejected: boolean;
  20 |     readonly isCancelled: boolean;
  21 | 
  22 |     (cancelHandler: () => void): void;
  23 | }
  24 | 
  25 | export class CancelablePromise<T> implements Promise<T> {
  26 |     #isResolved: boolean;
  27 |     #isRejected: boolean;
  28 |     #isCancelled: boolean;
  29 |     readonly #cancelHandlers: (() => void)[];
  30 |     readonly #promise: Promise<T>;
  31 |     #resolve?: (value: T | PromiseLike<T>) => void;
  32 |     #reject?: (reason?: any) => void;
  33 | 
  34 |     constructor(
  35 |         executor: (
  36 |             resolve: (value: T | PromiseLike<T>) => void,
  37 |             reject: (reason?: any) => void,
  38 |             onCancel: OnCancel
  39 |         ) => void
  40 |     ) {
  41 |         this.#isResolved = false;
  42 |         this.#isRejected = false;
  43 |         this.#isCancelled = false;
  44 |         this.#cancelHandlers = [];
  45 |         this.#promise = new Promise<T>((resolve, reject) => {
  46 |             this.#resolve = resolve;
  47 |             this.#reject = reject;
  48 | 
  49 |             const onResolve = (value: T | PromiseLike<T>): void => {
  50 |                 if (this.#isResolved || this.#isRejected || this.#isCancelled) {
  51 |                     return;
  52 |                 }
  53 |                 this.#isResolved = true;
  54 |                 if (this.#resolve) this.#resolve(value);
  55 |             };
  56 | 
  57 |             const onReject = (reason?: any): void => {
  58 |                 if (this.#isResolved || this.#isRejected || this.#isCancelled) {
  59 |                     return;
  60 |                 }
  61 |                 this.#isRejected = true;
  62 |                 if (this.#reject) this.#reject(reason);
  63 |             };
  64 | 
  65 |             const onCancel = (cancelHandler: () => void): void => {
  66 |                 if (this.#isResolved || this.#isRejected || this.#isCancelled) {
  67 |                     return;
  68 |                 }
  69 |                 this.#cancelHandlers.push(cancelHandler);
  70 |             };
  71 | 
  72 |             Object.defineProperty(onCancel, 'isResolved', {
  73 |                 get: (): boolean => this.#isResolved,
  74 |             });
  75 | 
  76 |             Object.defineProperty(onCancel, 'isRejected', {
  77 |                 get: (): boolean => this.#isRejected,
  78 |             });
  79 | 
  80 |             Object.defineProperty(onCancel, 'isCancelled', {
  81 |                 get: (): boolean => this.#isCancelled,
  82 |             });
  83 | 
  84 |             return executor(onResolve, onReject, onCancel as OnCancel);
  85 |         });
  86 |     }
  87 | 
  88 |     get [Symbol.toStringTag]() {
  89 |         return "Cancellable Promise";
  90 |     }
  91 | 
  92 |     public then<TResult1 = T, TResult2 = never>(
  93 |         onFulfilled?: ((value: T) => TResult1 | PromiseLike<TResult1>) | null,
  94 |         onRejected?: ((reason: any) => TResult2 | PromiseLike<TResult2>) | null
  95 |     ): Promise<TResult1 | TResult2> {
  96 |         return this.#promise.then(onFulfilled, onRejected);
  97 |     }
  98 | 
  99 |     public catch<TResult = never>(
 100 |         onRejected?: ((reason: any) => TResult | PromiseLike<TResult>) | null
 101 |     ): Promise<T | TResult> {
 102 |         return this.#promise.catch(onRejected);
 103 |     }
 104 | 
 105 |     public finally(onFinally?: (() => void) | null): Promise<T> {
 106 |         return this.#promise.finally(onFinally);
 107 |     }
 108 | 
 109 |     public cancel(): void {
 110 |         if (this.#isResolved || this.#isRejected || this.#isCancelled) {
 111 |             return;
 112 |         }
 113 |         this.#isCancelled = true;
 114 |         if (this.#cancelHandlers.length) {
 115 |             try {
 116 |                 for (const cancelHandler of this.#cancelHandlers) {
 117 |                     cancelHandler();
 118 |                 }
 119 |             } catch (error) {
 120 |                 console.warn('Cancellation threw an error', error);
 121 |                 return;
 122 |             }
 123 |         }
 124 |         this.#cancelHandlers.length = 0;
 125 |         if (this.#reject) this.#reject(new CancelError('Request aborted'));
 126 |     }
 127 | 
 128 |     public get isCancelled(): boolean {
 129 |         return this.#isCancelled;
 130 |     }
 131 | }

  32 |         typeof value.stream === 'function' &&

  58 | export const getQueryString = (params: Record<string, any>): string => {
  59 |     const qs: string[] = [];
  60 | 
  61 |     const append = (key: string, value: any) => {
  62 |         qs.push(`${encodeURIComponent(key)}=${encodeURIComponent(String(value))}`);
  63 |     };
  64 | 
  65 |     const process = (key: string, value: any) => {
  66 |         if (isDefined(value)) {
  67 |             if (Array.isArray(value)) {
  68 |                 value.forEach(v => {
  69 |                     process(key, v);
  70 |                 });
  71 |             } else if (typeof value === 'object') {
  72 |                 Object.entries(value).forEach(([k, v]) => {
  73 |                     process(`${key}[${k}]`, v);
  74 |                 });
  75 |             } else {
  76 |                 append(key, value);
  77 |             }
  78 |         }
  79 |     };
  80 | 
  81 |     Object.entries(params).forEach(([key, value]) => {
  82 |         process(key, value);
  83 |     });
  84 | 
  85 |     if (qs.length > 0) {
  86 |         return `?${qs.join('&')}`;
  87 |     }
  88 | 
  89 |     return '';
  90 | };
  91 | 
  92 | const getUrl = (config: OpenAPIConfig, options: ApiRequestOptions): string => {
  93 |     const encoder = config.ENCODE_PATH || encodeURI;
  94 | 
  95 |     const path = options.url
  96 |         .replace('{api-version}', config.VERSION)
  97 |         .replace(/{(.*?)}/g, (substring: string, group: string) => {
  98 |             if (options.path?.hasOwnProperty(group)) {
  99 |                 return encoder(String(options.path[group]));
 100 |             }
 101 |             return substring;
 102 |         });
 103 | 
 104 |     const url = `${config.BASE}${path}`;
 105 |     if (options.query) {
 106 |         return `${url}${getQueryString(options.query)}`;
 107 |     }
 108 |     return url;
 109 | };

 111 | export const getFormData = (options: ApiRequestOptions): FormData | undefined => {
 112 |     if (options.formData) {
 113 |         const formData = new FormData();
 114 | 
 115 |         const process = (key: string, value: any) => {
 116 |             if (isString(value) || isBlob(value)) {
 117 |                 formData.append(key, value);
 118 |             } else {
 119 |                 formData.append(key, JSON.stringify(value));
 120 |             }
 121 |         };
 122 | 
 123 |         Object.entries(options.formData)
 124 |             .filter(([_, value]) => isDefined(value))
 125 |             .forEach(([key, value]) => {
 126 |                 if (Array.isArray(value)) {
 127 |                     value.forEach(v => process(key, v));
 128 |                 } else {
 129 |                     process(key, value);
 130 |                 }
 131 |             });
 132 | 
 133 |         return formData;
 134 |     }
 135 |     return undefined;
 136 | };

 140 | export const resolve = async <T>(options: ApiRequestOptions, resolver?: T | Resolver<T>): Promise<T | undefined> => {
 141 |     if (typeof resolver === 'function') {
 142 |         return (resolver as Resolver<T>)(options);

 144 |     return resolver;

 147 | export const getHeaders = async (config: OpenAPIConfig, options: ApiRequestOptions, formData?: FormData): Promise<Record<string, string>> => {
 148 |     const [token, username, password, additionalHeaders] = await Promise.all([
 149 |         resolve(options, config.TOKEN),
 150 |         resolve(options, config.USERNAME),
 151 |         resolve(options, config.PASSWORD),
 152 |         resolve(options, config.HEADERS),
 153 |     ]);
 154 | 
 155 |     const formHeaders = typeof formData?.getHeaders === 'function' && formData?.getHeaders() || {}
 156 | 
 157 |     const headers = Object.entries({
 158 |         Accept: 'application/json',
 159 |         ...additionalHeaders,
 160 |         ...options.headers,
 161 |         ...formHeaders,
 162 |     })
 163 |     .filter(([_, value]) => isDefined(value))
 164 |     .reduce((headers, [key, value]) => ({
 165 |         ...headers,
 166 |         [key]: String(value),
 167 |     }), {} as Record<string, string>);
 168 | 
 169 |     if (isStringWithValue(token)) {
 170 |         headers['Authorization'] = `Bearer ${token}`;
 171 |     }
 172 | 
 173 |     if (isStringWithValue(username) && isStringWithValue(password)) {
 174 |         const credentials = base64(`${username}:${password}`);
 175 |         headers['Authorization'] = `Basic ${credentials}`;
 176 |     }
 177 | 
 178 |     if (options.body !== undefined) {
 179 |         if (options.mediaType) {
 180 |             headers['Content-Type'] = options.mediaType;
 181 |         } else if (isBlob(options.body)) {
 182 |             headers['Content-Type'] = options.body.type || 'application/octet-stream';
 183 |         } else if (isString(options.body)) {
 184 |             headers['Content-Type'] = 'text/plain';
 185 |         } else if (!isFormData(options.body)) {
 186 |             headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json';
 187 |         }
 188 |     }
 189 | 
 190 |     return headers;
 191 | };

 193 | export const getRequestBody = (options: ApiRequestOptions): any => {

 195 |         return options.body;
 196 |     }
 197 |     return undefined;

 200 | export const sendRequest = async <T>(
 201 |     config: OpenAPIConfig,
 202 |     options: ApiRequestOptions,
 203 |     url: string,
 204 |     body: any,
 205 |     formData: FormData | undefined,
 206 |     headers: Record<string, string>,
 207 |     onCancel: OnCancel,
 208 |     axiosClient: AxiosInstance
 209 | ): Promise<AxiosResponse<T>> => {
 210 |     const source = axios.CancelToken.source();
 211 | 
 212 |     const requestConfig: AxiosRequestConfig = {
 213 |         url,
 214 |         headers,
 215 |         data: body ?? formData,
 216 |         method: options.method,
 217 |         withCredentials: config.WITH_CREDENTIALS,
 218 |         withXSRFToken: config.CREDENTIALS === 'include' ? config.WITH_CREDENTIALS : false,
 219 |         cancelToken: source.token,
 220 |     };
 221 | 
 222 |     onCancel(() => source.cancel('The user aborted a request.'));
 223 | 
 224 |     try {
 225 |         return await axiosClient.request(requestConfig);
 226 |     } catch (error) {
 227 |         const axiosError = error as AxiosError<T>;
 228 |         if (axiosError.response) {
 229 |             return axiosError.response;
 230 |         }
 231 |         throw error;
 232 |     }
 233 | };

 249 |     return undefined;

 252 | export const catchErrorCodes = (options: ApiRequestOptions, result: ApiResult): void => {
 253 |     const errors: Record<number, string> = {
 254 |         400: 'Bad Request',
 255 |         401: 'Unauthorized',
 256 |         403: 'Forbidden',
 257 |         404: 'Not Found',
 258 |         500: 'Internal Server Error',
 259 |         502: 'Bad Gateway',
 260 |         503: 'Service Unavailable',
 261 |         ...options.errors,
 262 |     }
 263 | 
 264 |     const error = errors[result.status];
 265 |     if (error) {
 266 |         throw new ApiError(options, result, error);
 267 |     }
 268 | 
 269 |     if (!result.ok) {
 270 |         const errorStatus = result.status ?? 'unknown';
 271 |         const errorStatusText = result.statusText ?? 'unknown';
 272 |         const errorBody = (() => {
 273 |             try {
 274 |                 return JSON.stringify(result.body, null, 2);
 275 |             } catch (e) {
 276 |                 return undefined;
 277 |             }
 278 |         })();
 279 | 
 280 |         throw new ApiError(options, result,
 281 |             `Generic Error: status: ${errorStatus}; status text: ${errorStatusText}; body: ${errorBody}`
 282 |         );
 283 |     }
 284 | };
 285 | 
 286 | /**
 287 |  * Request method
 288 |  * @param config The OpenAPI configuration object
 289 |  * @param options The request options from the service
 290 |  * @param axiosClient The axios client instance to use
 291 |  * @returns CancelablePromise<T>
 292 |  * @throws ApiError
 293 |  */
 294 | export const request = <T>(config: OpenAPIConfig, options: ApiRequestOptions, axiosClient: AxiosInstance = axios): CancelablePromise<T> => {
 295 |     return new CancelablePromise(async (resolve, reject, onCancel) => {
 296 |         try {
 297 |             const url = getUrl(config, options);
 298 |             const formData = getFormData(options);
 299 |             const body = getRequestBody(options);
 300 |             const headers = await getHeaders(config, options, formData);
 301 | 
 302 |             if (!onCancel.isCancelled) {
 303 |                 const response = await sendRequest<T>(config, options, url, body, formData, headers, onCancel, axiosClient);
 304 |                 const responseBody = getResponseBody(response);
 305 |                 const responseHeader = getResponseHeader(response, options.responseHeader);
 306 | 
 307 |                 const result: ApiResult = {
 308 |                     url,
 309 |                     ok: isSuccess(response.status),
 310 |                     status: response.status,
 311 |                     statusText: response.statusText,
 312 |                     body: responseHeader ?? responseBody,
 313 |                 };
 314 | 
 315 |                 catchErrorCodes(options, result);
 316 | 
 317 |                 resolve(result.body);
 318 |             }
 319 |         } catch (error) {
 320 |             reject(error);
 321 |         }
 322 |     });
 323 | };

   1 | /* FILEPATH: frontend/src/config.ts */
   2 | /* @file Application Configuration (The Environment Context) */
   3 | /* @author The Engineer */
   4 | /* @description Centralizes environment variables and base URLs.
   5 |  * FEATURES:
   6 |  * - âš¡ AUTO-DETECTION: Reads VITE_API_URL or defaults to localhost:8000.
   7 |  * - âš¡ NORMALIZATION: Strips trailing slashes AND '/api/v1' to prevent double-pathing.
   8 |  */
   9 | 
  10 | // 1. Detect API Base URL
  11 | // In Prod: Injected by CI/CD. In Dev: Defaults to Python backend port.
  12 | const RAW_API_URL = import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL || 'http://localhost:8000';
  13 | 
  14 | // 2. Normalize (Strip trailing slash and specific API suffix if present)
  15 | // This ensures we always get the HOST root (e.g. http://localhost:8000)
  16 | // even if the user set VITE_API_URL="http://localhost:8000/api/v1"
  17 | export const API_BASE_URL = RAW_API_URL
  18 |     .replace(/\/api\/v1\/?$/, '') // Remove /api/v1 if it was included in the env var
  19 |     .replace(/\/+$/, '');          // Remove any remaining trailing slashes
  20 | 
  21 | // 3. Application Metadata
  22 | export const APP_VERSION = import.meta.env.VITE_APP_VERSION || '2.5.0';
  23 | export const IS_DEV = import.meta.env.DEV;
  24 | export const IS_DEBUG = import.meta.env.VITE_DEBUG_MODE === 'true';

# Source code from: frontend\src\domains\meta\_kernel\MetaContext.tsx
-----------------------------------------------------------------------
   1 | // FILEPATH: frontend/src/domains/meta/_kernel/MetaContext.tsx
   2 | // @file: Meta Context (The Brain)
   3 | // @role: ðŸ§  State Manager */
   4 | // @author: The Engineer
   5 | // @description: Manages Domain Selection, Scope, and Deep Linking. Bridges the URL to the Application State.
   6 | // @security-level: LEVEL 0 (Kernel) */
   7 | 
   8 | import React, { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useMemo } from 'react';
   9 | import { useUrlState } from '../../../platform/hooks/useUrlState';
  10 | import { logger } from '../../../platform/logging/Narrator';
  11 | import { MetaKernelService } from '../../../api/services/MetaKernelService';
  12 | import { useQuery } from '@tanstack/react-query';
  13 | 
  14 | // âš¡ CRITICAL FIX: IMPORT SHARED CONTRACTS AS TYPES ONLY
  15 | import type { 
  16 |     MetaContextState, 
  17 |     DomainSummary, 
  18 |     ScopeSummary 
  19 | } from '../types';
  20 | 
  21 | // Default State (Safe Fallback)
  22 | const DEFAULT_STATE: MetaContextState = {
  23 |     selectedDomain: null,
  24 |     selectedScope: null,
  25 |     selectedItem: null,
  26 |     domains: [],
  27 |     isLoading: true,
  28 |     error: null,
  29 |     selectDomain: () => logger.scream("META", "selectDomain called before Context Init"),
  30 |     selectScope: () => {},
  31 |     selectItem: () => {},
  32 |     refresh: () => {}
  33 | };
  34 | 
  35 | const MetaContext = createContext<MetaContextState>(DEFAULT_STATE);
  36 | 
  37 | export const MetaProvider: React.FC<{ children: React.ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {
  38 |     
  39 |     // 1. DATA: Fetch Topology (Domains -> Scopes)
  40 |     const { 
  41 |         data: rawDomains = [], 
  42 |         isLoading, 
  43 |         error, 
  44 |         refetch 
  45 |     } = useQuery({
  46 |         queryKey: ['meta', 'domains'],
  47 |         queryFn: async () => {
  48 |             logger.tell("META", "ðŸ“¡ Fetching System Topology...");
  49 |             // âš¡ API FIX: Match the exact generated OpenAPI SDK method name
  50 |             const response = await MetaKernelService.listDomainsApiV1MetaDomainsGet();
  51 |             
  52 |             // @ts-ignore - Handle Manifest Wrapper if present
  53 |             const domains = (response.modules || response) as DomainSummary[]; 
  54 |             logger.trace("META", "Topology Fetched", { count: domains?.length });
  55 |             return domains;
  56 |         },
  57 |         staleTime: 1000 * 60 * 5, 
  58 |     });
  59 | 
  60 |     // 2. STATE: Universal URL Persistence
  61 |     const [domainKey, setDomainKey] = useUrlState('domain', '');
  62 |     const [scopeKey, setScopeKey] = useUrlState('scope', '');
  63 |     const [itemId, setItemId] = useUrlState('select', ''); 
  64 | 
  65 |     // 3. DERIVED STATE: Resolve Objects from Keys
  66 |     const selectedDomain = useMemo(() => {
  67 |         if (!domainKey) return null;
  68 |         return rawDomains.find(d => d.key === domainKey) || null;
  69 |     }, [domainKey, rawDomains]);
  70 | 
  71 |     const selectedScope = useMemo(() => {
  72 |         if (!selectedDomain || !scopeKey) return null;
  73 |         return selectedDomain.scopes?.find(s => s.key === scopeKey) || null;
  74 |     }, [selectedDomain, scopeKey]);
  75 | 
  76 |     // 4. ACTIONS (The Interface Implementation)
  77 |     const selectDomain = (key: string) => {
  78 |         if (key === domainKey) return; 
  79 |         logger.tell("META", `ðŸ‘‰ Select Domain: ${key || 'None'}`);
  80 |         setDomainKey(key || null);
  81 |         // Clear children when parent changes
  82 |         setScopeKey(null);
  83 |         setItemId(null); 
  84 |     };
  85 | 
  86 |     const selectScope = (key: string) => {
  87 |         if (key === scopeKey) return;
  88 |         logger.tell("META", `ðŸ‘‰ Select Scope: ${key || 'None'}`);
  89 |         setScopeKey(key || null);
  90 |         setItemId(null);
  91 |     };
  92 | 
  93 |     const selectItem = (id: string | null) => {
  94 |         if (id === itemId) return;
  95 |         if (id) logger.tell("META", `ðŸ‘‰ Select Item: ${id}`);
  96 |         setItemId(id || null);
  97 |     };
  98 | 
  99 |     // 5. SIDE EFFECTS
 100 |     useEffect(() => {
 101 |         if (rawDomains.length > 0) {
 102 |             logger.whisper("META", `ðŸ“¥ Loaded ${rawDomains.length} Domains into Context`);
 103 |         }
 104 |     }, [rawDomains.length]);
 105 | 
 106 |     useEffect(() => {
 107 |         if (error) {
 108 |             logger.scream("META", "ðŸ”¥ Failed to fetch topology", error);
 109 |         }
 110 |     }, [error]);
 111 | 
 112 |     // 6. CONSTRUCT CONTEXT
 113 |     const value: MetaContextState = {
 114 |         domains: rawDomains,
 115 |         isLoading,
 116 |         error: error ? String(error) : null,
 117 |         selectedDomain,
 118 |         selectedScope,
 119 |         selectedItem: itemId,
 120 |         selectDomain,
 121 |         selectScope,
 122 |         selectItem,
 123 |         refresh: refetch
 124 |     };
 125 | 
 126 |     return (
 127 |         <MetaContext.Provider value={value}>
 128 |             {children}
 129 |         </MetaContext.Provider>
 130 |     );
 131 | };
 132 | 
 133 | export const useMetaContext = () => {
 134 |     const context = useContext(MetaContext);
 135 |     if (!context) {
 136 |         throw new Error("useMetaContext must be used within a MetaProvider");
 137 |     }
 138 |     return context;
 139 | };

  18 |     PlusOutlined,
  19 |     MenuFoldOutlined,
  20 |     MenuUnfoldOutlined
  21 | } from '@ant-design/icons';
  22 | import { useSearchParams } from 'react-router-dom';
  23 | 
  24 | // âš¡ SHARED COMPONENTS
  25 | import { DomainTree } from '../../components/DomainTree'; 
  26 | import { useMetaContext } from '../../_kernel/MetaContext';
  27 | import { useDomains } from '../../features/states/hooks/useDomains'; 
  28 | 
  29 | // Local Components
  30 | import { AttributeExplorer } from './components/AttributeExplorer';
  31 | import { AttributeEditor } from './components/AttributeEditor';
  32 | import { useDictionary } from './hooks/useDictionary';
  33 | 
  34 | // âš¡ CRITICAL FIX: Explicit type import to prevent Vite transpilation crash
  35 | import type { AttributeDraft } from './types/types'; 
  36 | 
  37 | import { AttributeType, WidgetType } from './types/constants'; // Explicit Import for Defaults (Enums exist at runtime)
  38 | 
  39 | // âš¡ CRITICAL FIX: Adjusted relative path depth (added one '../')
  40 | import { logger } from '../../../../platform/logging/Narrator'; 
  41 | 
  42 | const { Content, Sider } = Layout;
  43 | const { Title } = Typography;
  44 | 
  45 | // âš¡ SAFETY: Local Default to prevent "Undefined" crash.
  46 | // âš¡ CONTRACT FIX: Renamed 'config' -> 'configuration' to match Types.
  47 | const FRESH_DRAFT: AttributeDraft = {
  48 |     key: "",
  49 |     label: "",
  50 |     data_type: AttributeType.TEXT,
  51 |     widget_type: WidgetType.INPUT,
  52 |     is_system: false,
  53 |     is_dynamic: true,
  54 |     is_required: false,
  55 |     is_unique: false,
  56 |     is_active: true,
  57 |     options: [],
  58 |     configuration: {}, // âœ… CORRECT PROPERTY NAME
  59 |     domain: ""
  60 | };
  61 | 
  62 | export const DictionaryView: React.FC = () => {
  63 |     const { token } = theme.useToken();
  64 |     const [searchParams, setSearchParams] = useSearchParams();
  65 |     
  66 |     // 1. GLOBAL CONTEXT
  67 |     const { 
  68 |         selectedDomain, 
  69 |         selectDomain,
  70 |         selectedItem,
  71 |         selectItem 
  72 |     } = useMetaContext();
  73 | 
  74 |     const { domains, isLoading: isDomainsLoading } = useDomains();
  75 |     const domainKey = searchParams.get('domain');
  76 |     
  77 |     // Sync URL -> Context
  78 |     useEffect(() => {
  79 |         if (domainKey && (!selectedDomain || selectedDomain.key !== domainKey)) {
  80 |             if (domains.length > 0) selectDomain(domainKey);
  81 |         } else if (!domainKey && selectedDomain) {
  82 |             selectDomain('');
  83 |         }
  84 |     }, [domainKey, domains, selectedDomain]);
  85 | 
  86 |     // 2. FEATURE LOGIC
  87 |     const activeDomain = selectedDomain?.key || null;
  88 | 
  89 |     const { 
  90 |         attributes, 
  91 |         isLoading: isSchemaLoading, 
  92 |         saveAttribute, 
  93 |         deleteAttribute,
  94 |         refresh 
  95 |     } = useDictionary(activeDomain || '');
  96 | 
  97 |     // Local UI State
  98 |     const [collapsed, setCollapsed] = useState(false);
  99 |     const [isCreating, setIsCreating] = useState(false);
 100 |     
 101 |     // 3. HANDLERS
 102 |     const handleDomainSelect = (key: string) => {
 103 |         selectDomain(key);
 104 |         setSearchParams({ domain: key });
 105 |         setIsCreating(false);
 106 |     };
 107 | 
 108 |     const handleBack = () => {
 109 |         selectDomain('');
 110 |         setSearchParams({});
 111 |         selectItem(null);
 112 |         setIsCreating(false);
 113 |     };
 114 | 
 115 |     const handleEdit = (fieldKey: string) => {
 116 |         logger.tell("DICTIONARY", `âœï¸ Editing Field: ${fieldKey}`);
 117 |         selectItem(fieldKey);
 118 |         setIsCreating(false);
 119 |     };
 120 | 
 121 |     const handleCreate = () => {
 122 |         logger.tell("DICTIONARY", "âœ¨ Creating New Field");
 123 |         selectItem(null);
 124 |         setIsCreating(true);
 125 |     };
 126 | 
 127 |     const handleSave = async (draft: AttributeDraft) => {
 128 |         const success = await saveAttribute(draft);
 129 |         if (success) {
 130 |             setIsCreating(false);
 131 |             selectItem(null); 
 132 |         }
 133 |     };
 134 | 
 135 |     const handleDelete = async (key: string) => {
 136 |         const success = await deleteAttribute(key);
 137 |         if (success) {
 138 |             if (selectedItem === key) {
 139 |                 selectItem(null);
 140 |                 setIsCreating(false);
 141 |             }
 142 |         }
 143 |     };
 144 | 
 145 |     // 4. COMPUTED: Safe Data Resolution
 146 |     const activeDraft = useMemo(() => {
 147 |         if (selectedItem) {
 148 |             const found = attributes.find(a => a.key === selectedItem);
 149 |             if (found) {
 150 |                 return {
 151 |                     ...FRESH_DRAFT, // Use safe defaults for missing props
 152 |                     ...found,       // Overwrite with DB data
 153 |                     // âš¡ CONTRACT FIX: Ensure we map DB config to 'configuration'
 154 |                     configuration: found.configuration || (found as any).config || {}, 
 155 |                     domain: activeDomain || ''
 156 |                 } as AttributeDraft;
 157 |             }
 158 |         }
 159 |         
 160 |         // Return Fresh Draft for "New" mode
 161 |         return { 
 162 |             ...FRESH_DRAFT, 
 163 |             domain: activeDomain || '' 
 164 |         };
 165 |     }, [selectedItem, attributes, activeDomain]);
 166 | 
 167 |     // âš¡ SECURITY CHECK: Is this a System Field?
 168 |     const isSystemField = activeDraft.is_system;
 169 | 
 170 |     // âš¡ STATE: Are we in "New Mode"? 
 171 |     const isNewMode = isCreating || !selectedItem;
 172 | 
 173 |     // --- RENDER: STATE A (LOBBY) ---
 174 |     if (!activeDomain) {
 175 |         return (
 176 |             <div style={{ padding: 48, minHeight: '100%', background: token.colorBgLayout }}>
 177 |                 {isDomainsLoading ? (
 178 |                     <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', marginTop: 100 }}>
 179 |                          <Spin size="large" tip="Loading System Topology..." />
 180 |                     </div>
 181 |                 ) : (
 182 |                     <DomainTree 
 183 |                          domains={domains} 
 184 |                         onSelect={handleDomainSelect} 
 185 |                         isLoading={isDomainsLoading} 
 186 |                     />
 187 |                 )}
 188 |             </div>
 189 |         );
 190 |     }
 191 | 
 192 |     // --- RENDER: STATE B (MASTER-DETAIL EDITOR) ---
 193 |     const showEditor = selectedItem !== null || isCreating;
 194 | 
 195 |     return (
 196 |         <Layout style={{ height: '100vh', overflow: 'hidden' }}>
 197 |             {/* HEADER */}
 198 |             <div style={{ 
 199 |                 padding: '0 24px', 
 200 |                 background: token.colorBgContainer, 
 201 |                 borderBottom: `1px solid ${token.colorBorderSecondary}`,
 202 |                 display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center',
 203 |                 height: 64,
 204 |                 flexShrink: 0
 205 |             }}>
 206 |                 <Space>
 207 |                     <Button icon={<ArrowLeftOutlined />} onClick={handleBack}>Back</Button>
 208 |                     <Breadcrumb items={[
 209 |                         { title: <Space><DatabaseOutlined /> Data Dictionary</Space> },
 210 |                         { title: selectedDomain?.label || activeDomain }
 211 |                     ]} />
 212 |                 </Space>
 213 |                 <Space>
 214 |                     <Button icon={<ReloadOutlined />} onClick={refresh} loading={isSchemaLoading}>Refresh</Button>
 215 |                     <Button type="primary" icon={<PlusOutlined />} onClick={handleCreate}>New Field</Button>
 216 |                 </Space>
 217 |             </div>
 218 | 
 219 |             {/* âš¡ LAYOUT FIX: 'hasSider' ensures Left-to-Right layout */}
 220 |             <Layout hasSider style={{ height: 'calc(100vh - 64px)' }}>
 221 |                 
 222 |                 {/* LEFT: ATTRIBUTE LIST */}
 223 |                 <Sider 
 224 |                     width={350} 
 225 |                     theme="light" 
 226 |                     collapsible 
 227 |                     collapsed={collapsed} 
 228 |                     trigger={null} // âš¡ FIX: Removed default bottom trigger
 229 |                     style={{ 
 230 |                         borderRight: `1px solid ${token.colorBorderSecondary}`,
 231 |                         overflowY: 'auto',
 232 |                         height: '100%',
 233 |                         zIndex: 10
 234 |                     }}
 235 |                 >
 236 |                     <div style={{ padding: 16 }}>
 237 |                         {/* âš¡ FIX: Header with Collapse Toggle */}
 238 |                         <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', marginBottom: 16 }}>
 239 |                             {!collapsed && <Title level={5} style={{ margin: 0 }}>Attributes</Title>}
 240 |                             <Button 
 241 |                                 type="text" 
 242 |                                 icon={collapsed ? <MenuUnfoldOutlined /> : <MenuFoldOutlined />} 
 243 |                                 onClick={() => setCollapsed(!collapsed)}
 244 |                             />
 245 |                         </div>
 246 | 
 247 |                         {isSchemaLoading ? (
 248 |                             <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', padding: 32 }}><Spin /></div>
 249 |                         ) : attributes.length === 0 ? (
 250 |                             <Empty description="No Attributes" image={Empty.PRESENTED_IMAGE_SIMPLE} />
 251 |                         ) : (
 252 |                             <AttributeExplorer 
 253 |                                 attributes={attributes} 
 254 |                                 onSelect={handleEdit}
 255 |                                 selectedKey={selectedItem}
 256 |                             />
 257 |                         )}
 258 |                     </div>
 259 |                 </Sider>
 260 | 
 261 |                 {/* RIGHT: EDITOR CANVAS */}
 262 |                 <Content style={{ 
 263 |                     padding: 24, 
 264 |                     overflowY: 'auto', 
 265 |                     height: '100%',
 266 |                     background: token.colorBgLayout
 267 |                 }}>
 268 |                     <div style={{ maxWidth: 800, margin: '0 auto', minHeight: '100%' }}>
 269 |                         {showEditor ? (
 270 |                             <div style={{ 
 271 |                                 background: token.colorBgContainer, 
 272 |                                 padding: 24, 
 273 |                                 borderRadius: token.borderRadiusLG,
 274 |                                 border: `1px solid ${token.colorBorderSecondary}`
 275 |                             }}>
 276 |                                 <AttributeEditor 
 277 |                                     // âš¡ KEY FIX: Force remount when switching items to reset form state
 278 |                                     key={selectedItem || 'new'} 
 279 |                                     draft={activeDraft}
 280 |                                     
 281 |                                     // âš¡ CRITICAL: Pass Mode Signal to Unlock Fields
 282 |                                     isNew={isNewMode}
 283 |                                     onSave={handleSave}
 284 | 
 285 |                                     // âš¡ SECURITY FIX: Disable delete for System Fields or New Items
 286 |                                     onDelete={(!isCreating && !isSystemField) ? () => handleDelete(selectedItem!) : undefined}
 287 |                                     isSaving={false} 
 288 |                                 />
 289 |                             </div>
 290 |                         ) : (
 291 |                             <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', marginTop: 100 }}>
 292 |                                 <Empty 
 293 |                                     description="Select a field to edit properties" 
 294 |                                     image={Empty.PRESENTED_IMAGE_SIMPLE} 
 295 |                                 >
 296 |                                     <Button type="primary" onClick={handleCreate}>Create New Field</Button>
 297 |                                 </Empty>
 298 |                             </div>
 299 |                         )}
 300 |                     </div>
 301 |                 </Content>
 302 |             </Layout>
 303 |         </Layout>
 304 |     );
 305 | };

  30 | interface AttributeEditorProps {

  32 |   isSaving: boolean;
  33 |   onSave: (draft: AttributeDraft) => void;
  34 |   onDelete?: () => void;
  35 |   isNew: boolean;
  36 | }
  37 | 
  38 | export const AttributeEditor: React.FC<AttributeEditorProps> = ({
  39 |   draft: initialDraft,
  40 |   isSaving,
  41 |   onSave,
  42 |   onDelete,
  43 |   isNew
  44 | }) => {
  45 |   useTrace('AttributeEditor', { id: initialDraft.id, type: initialDraft.data_type });
  46 | 
  47 |   const { token } = theme.useToken();
  48 |   const { activeDomain } = useMetaContext();
  49 |   
  50 |   const [localDraft, setLocalDraft] = useState<AttributeDraft>(initialDraft);
  51 |   
  52 |   // âš¡ SYNC: Update local state if parent selection changes
  53 |   useEffect(() => {
  54 |     setLocalDraft(initialDraft);
  55 |   }, [initialDraft.key, initialDraft.id]); // âš¡ DEPENDENCIES
  56 | 
  57 |   const isLocked = localDraft.is_system && !isNew;
  58 |   const compatibleWidgets = WIDGET_COMPATIBILITY[localDraft.data_type] || [WidgetType.INPUT];
  59 | 
  60 |   // âš¡ LOGIC: Auto-switch widget if data type changes
  61 |   useEffect(() => {
  62 |       if (!compatibleWidgets.includes(localDraft.widget_type)) {
  63 |           updateField('widget_type', compatibleWidgets[0]);
  64 |       }
  65 |   }, [localDraft.data_type]);
  66 | 
  67 |   const updateField = (field: keyof AttributeDraft, value: any) => {
  68 |       if (isLocked && field !== 'label' && field !== 'description') return; // Allow cosmetic edits
  69 |       setLocalDraft(prev => ({ ...prev, [field]: value }));
  70 |   };
  71 | 
  72 |   // âš¡ CONTRACT FIX: Updates 'configuration', NOT 'config'
  73 |   const updateConfig = (key: keyof AttributeConfig, value: any) => {
  74 |     // We allow config updates even if locked, generally (e.g. placeholder)
  75 |     // but maybe not logic. For now, allow it.
  76 |     setLocalDraft(prev => ({
  77 |       ...prev,
  78 |       configuration: {
  79 |         ...(prev.configuration || {}),
  80 |         [key]: value
  81 |       }
  82 |     }));
  83 |   };
  84 | 
  85 |   const handleLabelChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
  86 |     const label = e.target.value;
  87 |     if (isNew) {
  88 |         // âš¡ LOGIC: Auto-Slugify
  89 |         const key = label.toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9_]/g, '_');
  90 |         setLocalDraft(prev => ({ ...prev, label, key }));
  91 |     } else {
  92 |         updateField('label', label);
  93 |     }
  94 |   };
  95 | 
  96 |   return (
  97 |     <div style={{ paddingBottom: 48 }}>
  98 |         
  99 |         {/* 1. HEADER */}
 100 |         <div style={{ 
 101 |             display: 'flex', 
 102 |             justifyContent: 'space-between', 
 103 |             alignItems: 'center',
 104 |             marginBottom: 24
 105 |         }}>
 106 |             <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 12 }}>
 107 |                 <Typography.Title level={3} style={{ margin: 0, color: token.colorText }}>
 108 |                     {isNew ? 'New Attribute' : localDraft.label}
 109 |                 </Typography.Title>
 110 |                 {isLocked && <Tag icon={<LockOutlined />} color="warning">System Field</Tag>}
 111 |             </div>
 112 | 
 113 |             <Space>
 114 |                 {onDelete && !isLocked && (
 115 |                     <Button danger icon={<DeleteOutlined />} onClick={onDelete}>Delete</Button>
 116 |                 )}
 117 |                 
 118 |                 <Button 
 119 |                     type="primary" 
 120 |                     icon={<SaveOutlined />} 
 121 |                     loading={isSaving}
 122 |                     onClick={() => onSave(localDraft)}
 123 |                 >
 124 |                     Save Changes
 125 |                 </Button>
 126 |             </Space>
 127 |         </div>
 128 | 
 129 |         <Row gutter={24}>
 130 |             {/* 2. CONFIGURATION */}
 131 |             <Col span={14}>
 132 |                 <Form layout="vertical">
 133 |                     
 134 |                     {/* A. DEFINITION */}
 135 |                     <Card title="Definition" size="small" style={{ marginBottom: 24 }}>
 136 |                         <Row gutter={16}>
 137 |                             <Col span={12}>
 138 |                                 <Form.Item label="Label" required tooltip="The human-readable name shown in forms.">
 139 |                                     <Input 
 140 |                                         value={localDraft.label} 
 141 |                                         onChange={handleLabelChange} 
 142 |                                         // Label is editable even if locked (usually)
 143 |                                     />
 144 |                                 </Form.Item>
 145 |                             </Col>
 146 |                             <Col span={12}>
 147 |                                 <Form.Item label="Machine Key" required tooltip="The database column name. Must be unique within the domain.">
 148 |                                     <Input 
 149 |                                         value={localDraft.key} 
 150 |                                         disabled={!isNew} // âš¡ LOCK if not new
 151 |                                         style={{ fontFamily: 'monospace' }}
 152 |                                         prefix={!isNew ? <LockOutlined style={{ color: token.colorTextQuaternary }} /> : undefined}
 153 |                                     />
 154 |                                 </Form.Item>
 155 |                             </Col>
 156 |                         </Row>
 157 |                         <Form.Item label="Description">
 158 |                             <TextArea 
 159 |                                 rows={2} 
 160 |                                 value={localDraft.description} 
 161 |                                 onChange={e => updateField('description', e.target.value)}
 162 |                                 placeholder="Explain what this field is used for..."
 163 |                             />
 164 |                         </Form.Item>
 165 |                     </Card>
 166 | 
 167 |                     {/* B. LOGIC */}
 168 |                     <Card 
 169 |                         title={
 170 |                             <Space>
 171 |                                 <span>Data Logic</span>
 172 |                                 <Tooltip title={HELP_TEXT.DATA_TYPE.desc}>
 173 |                                     <QuestionCircleOutlined style={{ color: token.colorTextSecondary }} />
 174 |                                 </Tooltip>
 175 |                             </Space>
 176 |                         } 
 177 |                         size="small" 
 178 |                         style={{ marginBottom: 24 }}
 179 |                     >

 184 |                                         value={localDraft.data_type}
 185 |                                         onChange={v => updateField('data_type', v)}
 186 |                                         disabled={!isNew} // âš¡ LOCK if not new
 187 |                                     >
 188 |                                         {Object.values(AttributeType).map(t => (

  54 |         updatePolicy,
  55 |         deletePolicy,
  56 |         dryRunPolicy,
  57 |         isMutating
  58 |     } = useGovernance(selectedDomainKey || '');
  59 | 
  60 |     // 3. HANDLERS
  61 |     const handleDomainSelect = (key: string) => {
  62 |         setSelectedDomainKey(key);
  63 |     };
  64 | 
  65 |     const handleBackToLobby = () => {
  66 |         setSelectedDomainKey(null);
  67 |     };
  68 | 
  69 |     const handleSelectPolicy = (key: string) => {
  70 |         setSelectedItem(key);
  71 |     };
  72 | 
  73 |     const handleCreate = () => {
  74 |         setSelectedItem('NEW');
  75 |     };
  76 | 
  77 |     const handleSave = async (payload: any) => {
  78 |         if (selectedItem === 'NEW') {
  79 |             await createPolicy(payload);
  80 |         } else {
  81 |             const policy = policies?.find(p => p.key === selectedItem);
  82 |             if (policy) {
  83 |                 await updatePolicy(policy.id, payload);
  84 |             }
  85 |         }
  86 |         setSelectedItem(null);
  87 |     };
  88 | 
  89 |     const handleDelete = async (id: number) => {
  90 |         await deletePolicy(id);
  91 |         const policy = policies?.find(p => p.id === id);
  92 |         if (policy && policy.key === selectedItem) {
  93 |             setSelectedItem(null);
  94 |         }
  95 |     };
  96 | 
  97 |     // 4. COMPUTED
  98 |     const activeDraft = useMemo(() => {
  99 |         if (!selectedItem || selectedItem === 'NEW') return null;
 100 |         return policies?.find(p => p.key === selectedItem);
 101 |     }, [policies, selectedItem]);
 102 | 
 103 |     // --- RENDER: STATE A (LOBBY) ---
 104 |     if (!selectedDomainKey) {
 105 |         return (
 106 |             <FadeIn>
 107 |                 <div style={{ padding: 40, maxWidth: 1200, margin: '0 auto' }}>
 108 |                     <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', marginBottom: 40 }}>
 109 |                         <Title level={2}>
 110 |                             <Space>
 111 |                                 <SafetyCertificateOutlined style={{ color: token.colorWarning }} />
 112 |                                 Governance Engine
 113 |                             </Space>
 114 |                         </Title>
 115 |                         <Text type="secondary" style={{ fontSize: 16 }}>
 116 |                             Select a Domain to enforce Business Rules and Compliance Policies.
 117 |                         </Text>
 118 |                     </div>
 119 |                     
 120 |                     {isLoadingDomains ? (
 121 |                         <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', padding: 40 }}>
 122 |                             <Spin size="large" tip="Loading Registry..." />
 123 |                         </div>
 124 |                     ) : (
 125 |                         <DomainPicker 
 126 |                             domains={domainList} 
 127 |                             onSelect={handleDomainSelect} 
 128 |                         />
 129 |                     )}
 130 |                 </div>
 131 |             </FadeIn>
 132 |         );
 133 |     }
 134 | 
 135 |     // --- RENDER: STATE B (EDITOR) ---
 136 |     return (
 137 |         <FadeIn>
 138 |             <Layout style={{ height: 'calc(100vh - 60px)', overflow: 'hidden', background: token.colorBgLayout }}>
 139 |                 {/* LEFT PANEL: EXPLORER */}
 140 |                 <Sider 
 141 |                     width={340} 
 142 |                     theme="light" 
 143 |                     collapsible 
 144 |                     collapsed={!leftOpen} 
 145 |                     collapsedWidth={0} 
 146 |                     trigger={null}
 147 |                     style={{ 
 148 |                         borderRight: `1px solid ${token.colorBorderSecondary}`,
 149 |                         zIndex: 10
 150 |                     }}
 151 |                 >
 152 |                     <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', height: '100%' }}>
 153 |                         {/* HEADER */}
 154 |                         <div style={{ 
 155 |                             padding: 16, 
 156 |                             borderBottom: `1px solid ${token.colorSplit}`,
 157 |                             background: token.colorFillQuaternary 
 158 |                         }}>
 159 |                             <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8, marginBottom: 12 }}>
 160 |                                 <Tooltip title="Change Domain">
 161 |                                     <Button 
 162 |                                         type="text" 
 163 |                                         icon={<ArrowLeftOutlined />} 
 164 |                                         onClick={handleBackToLobby} 
 165 |                                         size="small"
 166 |                                     />
 167 |                                 </Tooltip>
 168 |                                 <BankOutlined style={{ color: token.colorWarning }} />
 169 |                                 <Text strong style={{ fontSize: 16, whiteSpace: 'nowrap', overflow: 'hidden', textOverflow: 'ellipsis' }}>
 170 |                                     {activeDomain?.label || selectedDomainKey}
 171 |                                 </Text>
 172 |                             </div>
 173 |                             <Button type="primary" block icon={<PlusOutlined />} onClick={handleCreate}>
 174 |                                 Draft Policy
 175 |                             </Button>
 176 |                         </div>
 177 |

 179 |                         <div style={{ flex: 1, overflow: 'hidden' }}>
 180 |                             <PolicyExplorer 
 181 |                                 policies={policies || []}
 182 |                                 selectedKey={selectedItem}
 183 |                                 onSelect={handleSelectPolicy}
 184 |                                 isLoading={isGovernanceLoading}
 185 |                                 searchTerm={searchTerm}
 186 |                                 onSearchChange={setSearchTerm}
 187 |                             />
 188 |                         </div>
 189 |                     </div>
 190 |                 </Sider>
 191 | 
 192 |                 {/* MAIN PANEL: EDITOR */}
 193 |                 <Content style={{ position: 'relative', height: '100%', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column' }}>
 194 |                     <FloatButton 
 195 |                         icon={leftOpen ? <MenuFoldOutlined /> : <MenuUnfoldOutlined />}
 196 |                         style={{ position: 'absolute', top: 16, left: 16, zIndex: 100 }}
 197 |                         onClick={() => setLeftOpen(!leftOpen)}
 198 |                     />
 199 | 
 200 |                     <div style={{ flex: 1, overflowY: 'auto', padding: 24 }}>
 201 |                         {selectedItem ? (
 202 |                             <PolicyEditor 
 203 |                                 key={selectedItem} // Force remount on switch
 204 |                                 draft={activeDraft || undefined}
 205 |                                 isNew={selectedItem === 'NEW'}
 206 |                                 onSave={handleSave}
 207 |                                 onDelete={handleDelete}
 208 |                                 onCancel={() => setSelectedItem(null)}
 209 |                                 isSaving={isMutating}
 210 |                                 onDryRun={dryRunPolicy}
 211 |                                 domain={activeDomain?.key || selectedDomainKey}
 212 |                             />
 213 |                         ) : (
 214 |                             <div style={{ height: '100%', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' }}>
 215 |                                 <Empty

 220 |                                 />
 221 |                             </div>
 222 |                         )}
 223 |                     </div>
 224 |                 </Content>

# Source code from: frontend\src\domains\meta\features\runner\RunnerView.tsx

   1 | // FILEPATH: frontend/src/domains/meta/features/runner/RunnerView.tsx
   2 | // @file: Process Runner Dashboard (Deep Linked + Smooth)
   3 | // @author: The Engineer
   4 | // @description: The "Launchpad" for Business Processes.
   5 | // REFACTOR: Implemented 'useUrlState' for Search Persistence.
   6 | // VISUAL: Added <FadeIn> wrapper for standard transitions.
   7 | // FEATURES:
   8 | // Discovery: Finds all 'WIZARD' scopes in the Registry.
   9 | // Filtering: Search by name or domain.
  10 | // Routing: Updates URL to launch RuntimeHost.
  11 | 
  12 | 
  13 | import React, { useMemo } from 'react';
  14 | import { useSearchParams } from 'react-router-dom';
  15 | import { ProList } from '@ant-design/pro-components';
  16 | import { theme, Typography, Tag, Button, Space, Card, Empty } from 'antd';
  17 | import { 
  18 |     RocketOutlined, 
  19 |     AppstoreOutlined,
  20 |     RightOutlined
  21 | } from '@ant-design/icons';
  22 | 
  23 | import { useMetaContext } from '../../_kernel/MetaContext';
  24 | import { RuntimeHost } from './RuntimeHost';
  25 | import { useUrlState } from '../../../../platform/hooks/useUrlState'; // âš¡ UNIVERSAL STATE
  26 | import { FadeIn } from '../../../../platform/ui/animation/FadeIn'; // âš¡ ANIMATION
  27 | 
  28 | const { Title, Text } = Typography;
  29 | 
  30 | export const RunnerView: React.FC = () => {
  31 |     const { token } = theme.useToken();
  32 |     const { domainList } = useMetaContext();
  33 |     const [searchParams, setSearchParams] = useSearchParams();
  34 |     
  35 |     // 1. UNIVERSAL URL STATE (Search Persistence)
  36 |     const [searchText, setSearchText] = useUrlState('q', '');
  37 | 
  38 |     // 2. DISCOVERY ENGINE
  39 |     // Flatten the Domain->Scope hierarchy into a list of "Apps"
  40 |     const availableApps = useMemo(() => {
  41 |         const apps: any[] = [];
  42 |         domainList.forEach(domain => {
  43 |             domain.scopes.forEach(scope => {
  44 |                 // âš¡ FILTER: Only show Wizards (Interactive Processes)
  45 |                 if (scope.type === 'WIZARD') {
  46 |                     apps.push({
  47 |                         id: `${domain.key}:${scope.key}`,
  48 |                         domain: domain.key,
  49 |                         scope: scope.key,
  50 |                         title: scope.label, // e.g. "New Employee Onboarding"
  51 |                         description: `Domain: ${domain.label}`,
  52 |                         avatar: domain.icon || 'ðŸ“¦',
  53 |                         type: scope.type
  54 |                     });
  55 |                 }
  56 |             });
  57 |         });
  58 |         return apps.filter(app => 
  59 |             app.title.toLowerCase().includes(searchText.toLowerCase()) ||
  60 |             app.domain.toLowerCase().includes(searchText.toLowerCase())
  61 |         );
  62 |     }, [domainList, searchText]);
  63 | 
  64 |     // 3. ROUTING LOGIC
  65 |     const activeDomain = searchParams.get('domain');
  66 |     const activeScope = searchParams.get('scope');
  67 |     const isRunning = !!(activeDomain && activeScope);
  68 | 
  69 |     const handleLaunch = (domain: string, scope: string) => {
  70 |         setSearchParams({ domain, scope });
  71 |     };
  72 | 
  73 |     const handleClose = () => {
  74 |         setSearchParams({});
  75 |     };
  76 | 
  77 |     // 4. RENDER: RUNTIME HOST (The Overlay)
  78 |     if (isRunning) {
  79 |         return (
  80 |             <RuntimeHost 
  81 |                 domain={activeDomain!} 
  82 |                 scope={activeScope!} 
  83 |                 onClose={handleClose} 
  84 |             />
  85 |         );
  86 |     }
  87 | 
  88 |     // 5. RENDER: DASHBOARD (The Grid)
  89 |     return (
  90 |         <FadeIn>
  91 |             <div style={{ padding: '24px 40px', maxWidth: 1400, margin: '0 auto' }}>
  92 |                 
  93 |                 <div style={{ marginBottom: 40, textAlign: 'center' }}>
  94 |                     <Title level={2}>
  95 |                         <Space>
  96 |                             <RocketOutlined style={{ color: token.colorPrimary }} />
  97 |                             Process Runner
  98 |                         </Space>
  99 |                     </Title>
 100 |                     <Text type="secondary" style={{ fontSize: 16 }}>
 101 |                         Select a workflow to initiate a new business process.
 102 |                     </Text>
 103 |                 </div>
 104 | 
 105 |                 <ProList<any>
 106 |                     grid={{ gutter: 24, column: 3, xs: 1, sm: 2, md: 2, lg: 3, xl: 3, xxl: 4 }}
 107 |                     dataSource={availableApps}
 108 |                     renderItem={(item) => (
 109 |                         <Card
 110 |                             hoverable
 111 |                             onClick={() => handleLaunch(item.domain, item.scope)}
 112 |                             style={{ 
 113 |                                 height: '100%', 
 114 |                                 borderRadius: token.borderRadiusLG,
 115 |                                 borderTop: `4px solid ${token.colorInfo}`
 116 |                             }}
 117 |                         >
 118 |                             <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'flex-start', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: 16 }}>
 119 |                                 <div style={{ 
 120 |                                     width: 48, height: 48, 
 121 |                                     background: token.colorFillAlter, 
 122 |                                     borderRadius: 12, 
 123 |                                     display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',
 124 |                                     fontSize: 24
 125 |                                 }}>
 126 |                                     {item.avatar}
 127 |                                 </div>
 128 |                                 <Tag color="purple">{item.type}</Tag>
 129 |                             </div>
 130 |                             
 131 |                             <Title level={5} style={{ marginBottom: 4 }}>{item.title}</Title>

   1 | // FILEPATH: frontend/src/domains/meta/features/states/StatesView.tsx
   2 | // @file: States View (Workflow Orchestrator)
   3 | // @role: ðŸŽ¨ UI Presentation */

  47 | 
  48 | const { Content, Sider } = Layout;
  49 | const { Title, Text } = Typography;
  50 | 
  51 | export const StatesView: React.FC = () => {
  52 |     const { token } = theme.useToken();
  53 |     const [searchParams, setSearchParams] = useSearchParams();
  54 | 
  55 |     // 1. GLOBAL CONTEXT (Deep Linking for Selection)
  56 |     const { 
  57 |         selectedDomain, 
  58 |         selectDomain, 
  59 |         selectScope,
  60 |         selectedScope,
  61 |         selectedItem,
  62 |         selectItem 
  63 |     } = useMetaContext();
  64 | 
  65 |     // Resolve active state from context (Handle DEFAULT case)
  66 |     const domainKey = selectedDomain?.key || null;
  67 |     const scopeKey = selectedScope?.key || null;
  68 | 
  69 |     // 2. UNIVERSAL URL STATE (Persistence)
  70 |     const urlDomain = searchParams.get('domain');
  71 |     const urlScope = searchParams.get('scope');
  72 |     const urlFilter = searchParams.get('filter'); // WIZARD | JOB | GOVERNANCE
  73 |     const urlNode = searchParams.get('node'); // âš¡ NODE SELECTION DEEP LINK (The "Amnesia" Cure)
  74 | 
  75 |     // Sync URL -> Context
  76 |     useEffect(() => {
  77 |         if (urlDomain && urlDomain !== domainKey) selectDomain(urlDomain);
  78 |         if (urlScope && urlScope !== scopeKey) selectScope(urlScope);
  79 |         
  80 |         // âš¡ NODE SYNC: If URL has node, sync to context. If URL has NO node, clear context.
  81 |         // We use '' to represent no selection in the URL, effectively null
  82 |         if (urlNode && urlNode !== selectedItem) {
  83 |             selectItem(urlNode);
  84 |         } else if (!urlNode && selectedItem) {
  85 |             selectItem(null);
  86 |         }
  87 |     }, [urlDomain, urlScope, urlNode]);
  88 | 
  89 |     // 3. DATA LOADING
  90 |     const { domains, isLoading: isDomainsLoading } = useDomains();
  91 |     
  92 |     // We only fetch workflows if a domain is selected
  93 |     const { 
  94 |         workflows, 
  95 |         isLoading: isWorkflowsLoading, 
  96 |         createWorkflow,
  97 |         updateWorkflow,
  98 |         deleteWorkflow,
  99 |         refresh: refreshWorkflows 
 100 |     } = useWorkflows(domainKey);
 101 | 
 102 |     // 4. Local UI State (Transient)
 103 |     const [isInspectorOpen, setIsInspectorOpen] = useState(false);
 104 |     const [isJsonDrawerOpen, setIsJsonDrawerOpen] = useState(false);
 105 |     const [isCreateModalOpen, setIsCreateModalOpen] = useState(false);
 106 | 
 107 |     // Auto-open right panel if we have a deep link selection
 108 |     useEffect(() => {
 109 |         if (selectedItem) setIsInspectorOpen(true);
 110 |     }, [selectedItem]);
 111 | 
 112 |     // Effect: Keep right panel sync with selection
 113 |     useEffect(() => {
 114 |         if (!isInspectorOpen && selectedItem) {
 115 |             // If panel closed but item selected, deselect item (two-way bind)
 116 |             selectItem(null);
 117 |             
 118 |             // Clean URL
 119 |             const newParams = new URLSearchParams(searchParams);
 120 |             newParams.delete('node');
 121 |             setSearchParams(newParams);
 122 |         }
 123 |     }, [isInspectorOpen]);
 124 | 
 125 | 
 126 |     // 5. Data Hooks
 127 |     // Find the definition for the selected scope
 128 |     const activeDefinition = useMemo(() => {
 129 |         if (!scopeKey) return null;
 130 |         return workflows.find(w => w.scope_key === scopeKey) || null;
 131 |     }, [workflows, scopeKey]);
 132 | 
 133 |     // âš¡ HELPER: Resolve Workflow Type Logic
 134 |     // We need to know if this is a WIZARD, JOB, or GOVERNANCE flow to render the right tools.
 135 |     const activeTypeInfo: WorkflowTypeDef | null = useMemo(() => {
 136 |         if (!activeDefinition && !scopeKey) return null;
 137 |         
 138 |         // A. Check Registry
 139 |         const registryScope = selectedDomain?.scopes.find(s => s.key === scopeKey);
 140 |         let typeKey = registryScope?.type || activeDefinition?.type;
 141 | 
 142 |         // B. Check Metadata
 143 |         if (!typeKey && activeDefinition?.meta?.type) {
 144 |             typeKey = activeDefinition.meta.type;
 145 |         }
 146 | 
 147 |         // C. Fallback
 148 |         if (!typeKey) typeKey = 'GOVERNANCE'; // Default
 149 | 
 150 |         // âš¡ SMART TYPE RESOLUTION
 151 |         // Some keys might be "WIZARD" (Backend enum) vs "WIZARD_FLOW" (UI Constant)
 152 |         // We normalize here.
 153 |         if (typeKey === 'WIZARD') return WORKFLOW_TYPES.WIZARD;
 154 |         if (typeKey === 'JOB') return WORKFLOW_TYPES.JOB;
 155 |         
 156 |         return WORKFLOW_TYPES.GOVERNANCE;
 157 |     }, [activeDefinition, selectedDomain, scopeKey]);
 158 | 
 159 | 
 160 |     // âš¡ FILTERED LIST
 161 |     const visibleWorkflows = useMemo(() => {
 162 |         if (!urlFilter) return workflows;
 163 |         return workflows.filter(w => w.type === urlFilter);
 164 |     }, [workflows, urlFilter]);
 165 | 
 166 | 
 167 |     // 6. Session Manager
 168 |     // Manages the "Draft" state vs "Live" state
 169 |     const session = useEditorSession(domainKey || '', scopeKey || '', activeDefinition);
 170 | 
 171 |     // 7. Navigation Guard
 172 |     const handleSelectWorkflow = (scope: string) => {
 173 |         if (scope === scopeKey) return; // No op
 174 |         selectScope(scope);
 175 |         setSearchParams({ domain: domainKey!, scope: scope }); // Keep filter if any? No, reset.
 176 |         
 177 |         // Close panels
 178 |         setIsInspectorOpen(false);
 179 |         selectItem(null);
 180 |     };
 181 | 
 182 |     const handleBack = () => {
 183 |         selectDomain('');
 184 |         setSearchParams({});
 185 |     };
 186 | 
 187 |     // If we have a domain but no scope selected, 
 188 |     // AND we have workflows, maybe auto-select the first one?
 189 |     // No, better to show a list/gallery view.
 190 |     useEffect(() => {
 191 |         if (domainKey && !scopeKey && workflows.length > 0) {
 192 |             // Optional: Auto-select first? 
 193 |             // handleSelectWorkflow(workflows[0].scope_key);
 194 |         }
 195 |     }, [domainKey, scopeKey, workflows]);
 196 | 
 197 |     // Sync Reset (If scope invalid for domain)
 198 |     useEffect(() => {
 199 |         if (scopeKey && !isWorkflowsLoading && workflows.length > 0) {
 200 |             const exists = workflows.find(w => w.scope_key === scopeKey);
 201 |             if (!exists) {
 202 |                 // Only reset if we are sure it's loaded and truly missing
 203 |                 // selectScope(''); // Commented out to prevent flash resets during load
 204 |             }
 205 |         }
 206 |     }, [scopeKey, workflows, isWorkflowsLoading]);
 207 | 
 208 |     // Canvas Update
 209 |     const onNodeSelect = (nodeId: string | null) => {
 210 |         logger.tell("FLOW", `ðŸ‘‡ Node Selected: ${nodeId}`);
 211 |         selectItem(nodeId);
 212 |         
 213 |         // Sync URL for F5 safety
 214 |         const newParams = new URLSearchParams(searchParams);
 215 |         if (nodeId) {
 216 |             newParams.set('node', nodeId);
 217 |             setIsInspectorOpen(true);
 218 |         } else {
 219 |             newParams.delete('node');
 220 |         }
 221 |         setSearchParams(newParams);
 222 |     };
 223 | 
 224 |     // --- RENDER: STATE A (LOBBY) ---
 225 |     if (!selectedDomain) {
 226 |         return (

 228 |                 {isDomainsLoading ? <Spin size="large" /> : (

 239 |             </div>

 241 |     }

 243 |     // --- RENDER: STATE B (WORKFLOW GALLERY) ---
